<Review>I wish I could give zero stars. I used to bring my kids here a couple years ago when we lived in Glendale and loved it. Once we moved right around the corner recently, I thought we'd be coming in all the time. But the only two times I've been since we moved to the area have been absolutely disappointing.

We came on the weekday before Independence Day holiday and were told they were closing early, though it didn't say so anywhere online or at the location. The lady said we could only stay 20 minutes but had to pay full price. My kids (2 and 4) were already crying so I paid and figured we'd be back soon and stay a long time to make up for it. I work full time now, so we finally got a chance to go yesterday. It was crazy hot out, but we walked anyway, thinking it would be all the better once we got inside and played in the AC. We arrived sweating and were turned away because they had a private party. The girl there (never seen her before, but could have been the owner, not sure) turned us away and threatened to call the cops when I started asking about their hours and whether they'd changed policies or owners because I had no idea they were "always closed on weekends" as she said. I told her the brochure I had from the last time I was there didn't say that (though it did have lots of prices crossed out and replaced in sharpie with higher costs, hmmmm). She said we couldn't even wait inside for my husband to pick us up in the car!

My kids were crying, we were all sweaty and upset, but I was simply asking about what had changed about policies, and she was threatening to call the cops?!?? So unnecessary and unprofessional. We were going to do my daughter's birthday there next month and I would have booked it today; I decided right then and there we won't be back again. We'll probably do Giggles and Hugs in Glendale instead, like last time.

Don't waste your time here unless you're prepared to be turned away at the door or kicked out within 20 minutes.

To add to the ordeal, they are now publicly lying, saying they never threatened to call the police when in fact they did so right away -- and more than once. Rude, unprofessional, and outrageous threats = NOT the kind of business I want to take my children to.

< review>
The technician was single minded in his assessment of the problem.  Black particles have been appearing routinely in our washing machine for the past 1-2 months. After spending an hour turning the machine on and off, and turning the water to the washer on and off, the technician insisted repeatedly that the problem was from "the water." He disregarded the fact that we have had our washer for more than 10-15 years, and never replaced the hoses!  He disregarded that the sink faucets right next to the washer ran totally clear water, but he repeatedly insisted the black particles "are from the water."
I don't think Sears makes it clear in the billing policy how customers are charged double. I thought the $139 for diagnosis included the time the technician was here to make a diagnosis.  The technician charged us $280.12 for the visit.  He was unable to come up with a plausible diagnosis, did not replace any parts, and provided no satisfactory solution. Both my wife and I surmised the black particles were from our old hoses, but for some reason the technician totally dismissed our theory. His explanation, "I have seen this before because of dirty water."
I would not recommend Sears home services repair to anyone based on this unsatisfactory encounter.  I am sorry to say that this technician is not good for your reputation.</review>

Pay $15 parking a day.

Pros:
Location

<rating>1<//rating>< text>
Looking for a delightfully loud, inconvenient, and dated room? Look no further than the Hotel Karlan by Hilton.

Listen, I actually prefer to stay at all Hilton Hotels over Marriott, and was looking forward to this "resort-like" retreat at a 4-star hotel to begin my honeymoon. My experience was far from resort-like, however, and I felt as though I would have been better off staying in a local City Motel with a blinking vacancy sign off a freeway somewhere (no offense if that's where you choose to stay).

Be forewarned first and foremost, you will need to carry your luggage up or down stairs (see pictures) depending where your room is. Although the front desk politely pointed me toward the elevator, what he failed to mention, is that my room (#325) was located across the complex down a set of stairs, where I had to scamper down a flight of stairs with four suit cases (wife included) without managing to topple over myself. Despite being extremely aggravated about the lack of heads up, I went about my evening.

The issues didn't stop there, unfortunately. Here are some other negatives with the hotel, besides being separated and inconvenient to access:
+ Gaps in the doors cause noise to flow right through to the room
+ The sliding door in the bathroom could prove it easier to move 14 cinder blocks than actually open the door
+ Shower door slams behind you--careful not to let it smack you on the way in
+ In the year 2018, we all have electronic devices (phones, tablets, watches, laptops), and in my business travels, I expect there to be plenty of outlets and if possible, USB plugs. This hotel has neither, with each device being a treasure hunt to find plugs hidden behind the bed, and no USB-accessible outlets.

Overall, this was an extremely disappointing start to our honeymoon vacation. I explained these issues to the front desk, and their compensation was to provide a free breakfast. Albeit helpful, it didn't solve the numerous issues and unpleasurable experience we had, so we decided to check out early move elsewhere.<//text>

I was coming into town for a wedding that started at 5pm. I arrived at 130 pm, but was told that early check was absolutely not available as they were completely booked from the night before. <Review>I stayed here for a week and it was fine and okay, but not my best stay due to several little annoyances. First, the a/c in the room doesn't seem to make a lot of sense. No matter what I set the thermostat to, it goes off at random times, albeit sometimes with a louder fan, and the room never seems to get to the temperature I set on the panel. Not sure how else to interpret it, but I would think when I set the thermostat to 70 it means I want the ambient temperature of the room to be 70, but it never felt that cool before the a/c would turn off. Too make up for this lack of cool, the mini fridge was actually a freezer, apparently. I was here for several days, so I stocked up on snacks and beverages, and they all froze, including the carbonated cans that burst... No knob to adjust the temperature seems to exist anywhere on the fridge unit. < text>
This place is gorgeous with amazing and serene views. It does not feel like a hotel, but more like a retreat. Our room was huge compared to other hotels I've stayed in, and the bathroom was well lit and accommodating. We had a courtyard room which offered a patio with table and chairs as well as a ceiling fan. It was private enough that we could set out there and really enjoy the relaxing view of open space, and our children had a place to play so they didn't feel cooped up all the time. This hotel is also conveniently located to shopping areas, lots of restaurants, and every destination we had planned to go to on our trip to San Diego. The pool is heated which was especially nice. There was also a hot tub, and both the pool and hot tub were clean and well taken care of. Large soft towels were also provided poolside as well as nice cabana style areas located around the pool. Room service, a gym, and office area also available. The staff were all so nice and went above and beyond to make sure our stay was well enjoyed. The place is on the pricier side, but well worth it to us. Although, we did find it odd that for as nice of a place as it is, and with how much money we were spending each night to stay there, we still had to pay for wifi! Other than that, we would not only recommend this place to everyone we know, we would also stay here again and again whenever we visit San Diego :-)< /text>

< review>
We NEEDED to get away as a family and reconnect.  For once there was no itinerary - except to sleep.  There were four of us in the room with 2 double beds - not queen like the web page advertises (the sheets are even labeled 'double'). The room was amazingly large with a balcony you could walk out onto, have a seat and enjoy. The beds are always comfortable, but it would be nice if they were actually queen sized. It was great having a sink outside of the bathroom, especially with two girls.  We all slept through the housekeeping staffs shift, they did call to check on us and see if we needed anything.  Once we listed our needed they were very quick to fill the list.  Sweet & helpful staff, gorgeous grounds, fantastic room, good price and great sleep - thee best!!!!  Having a grocery store across the street was an added bonus!

The only problem we encountered was on the second night when we requested a microwave.  After an hour and a half I called again to check the status.  The man who answered the phone (night shift employee) said he had already spoke with us to let us know that all the microwaves were being used - he gave a sassy sorry and he hung up.  Funny, I was sitting by the phone the entire time and the room phone NEVER rang.  Ticked me off, but I'll make sure it doesn't happen again.</review>

<Rating>5<//Rating><review>We stayed at this hotel for 6 nights in the past week and the experience was just amazing!

First, let me talk about why I booked this hotel in the first place. Originally I actually booked Marriott. After trying to call them to book a crib for my room for my baby and received extremely rude service over the phone (the person hung up on me after I questioned him about his rudeness over the phone), I cancelled my reservation with them and started looking elsewhere. Found this place on Expedia and the pictures looked amazing and the price was good so I booked it.

Property & Location:

The hotel is located right off Highway 15 and minutes away a shopping center with lots of shopping and restaurant options. The room is large and clean, very modern and nicely decorated. The only thing was our room only had a shower and no tub so it was a little difficult for us to bathe our two toddlers.

Service:

The staff is what made our trip unforgettable. Upon arrival, the front desk staff offered cookies and water to my two kids. They switched our room based on my needs and explained in detail where everything is located on the property. I was fully prepared to pay for the wireless internet but the lady waived the internet fee (we didn't end up getting charged anyway since we are HHonors members). Most importantly, seeing we have two young kids, the lady also gave us complimentary breakfast buffet vouchers for all 6 days that we stayed there!

Checking out was also extremely easy and efficient. I went to the front desk and provided my room number and it was all done. Although I have agreed to pay the $10/day parking, the front desk staff waived that for me as well!

Now onto our buffet breakfast service. The food selection was great with the traditional hot breakfast buffet and even smoked salmon. We were served by three different servers during our stay and all of them were quite pleasant and extremely attentive. They even remembered what we liked to drink after the first morning and brought our preferred drinks the next day. The only area of improvement in here is that the three servers all had different ideas on what's included in the complimentary breakfast voucher. The first server said we could order everything off of a la carte menu on top of the buffet. The next server said we are only allowed in the buffet and the third server said we can order off the menu but with limited selections. This was a little confusing but a minor problem since I only ate from the buffet anyway.

Overall, my family and I truly enjoyed the experience we had at Hotel Karlan and if we do ever go back to San Diego then that would be the hotel of choice.</review><Pics>None<//Pics>< response>
